ENTRY #311
================================================================================
[META]
API Key Used : #26

[INPUT]
Task  : Assess corner-wise exterior damage of Nalanda to evaluate localized structural weakness
Level : high
Target: Nalanda

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
[THINKING PROCESS]
1. Strategy Selection: The request is to "assess corner-wise exterior damage". This implies a focus on corners. The "URGENT" strategy is suitable for parallel processing of specific points.
2. Token Selection: The request explicitly mentions "corner-wise". There are 4 corners (A, B, C, D). The task also implies checking the walls connecting these corners for localized weakness. A reasonable decomposition would be to check each corner and the wall segment leading to it. This would be 4 corners + 4 walls = 8 tasks.
3. Pruning: The HARD LIMIT is 5 subtasks. The priority is Centroids > Walls > Corners.
    - Initial list: Corner A, Corner B, Corner C, Corner D, Wall AB, Wall BC, Wall CD, Wall DA. (8 tasks)
    - Pruning based on priority:
        - Keep Centroid (if applicable, not explicitly requested here, but good for overall context).
        - Keep Walls (4 tasks).
        - Keep Corners (4 tasks).
    - Total needed: 4 Walls + 4 Corners = 8 tasks.
    - To fit 5 tasks:
        - Priority: Centroid > Walls > Corners.
        - We need to drop 3 tasks.
        - Let's keep the 4 walls. That leaves 1 slot.
        - We can keep 1 corner. Which one? The prompt mentions "corner-wise" and "localized structural weakness". It doesn't specify *which* corner.
        - Alternative interpretation: "corner-wise" could mean checking *around* each corner. This implies checking the two walls meeting at each corner.
        - Let's re-evaluate: "Assess corner-wise exterior damage". This strongly suggests focusing on the corners themselves.
        - If we focus on corners, we can do 4 corners. That's 4 tasks.
